*sigh* he has such a way with words...
Each of Bill Wurtz's 3D songs has had it's own unique style.  Here Comes the Sun had a lot of shadows, and a lot of contrast. It was light against dark, and the music sounded very mysterious, while also being very hopeful. Like a sunrise over a dark world, which is exactly what the song is about I'm a Princess was nonsense. Nothing in the song made sense, and that was the point. It wasn't supposed to make sense. The shapes were very abstract, it was all up for interpretation. Got Some Money was very segmented and organized, despite being equally as abstract as all of Bill's songs. Very few of the visuals were complex, there was never too much to look at. One of the likely explanations for it's simplicity is that it never pans from scene to scene, unlike the first two 3D songs  More than a Dream is on a whole other level, though. It's got Bill's flagship abstract style, and it has plenty of nonsense, but there's only a couple of points in the song where it's difficult to understand the meaning. It's abstract, but it's clear. It's complex, but not busy. It's the Bill Wurtz style, perfected.  I can tell that Bill is finally comfortable in the 3D style.
